Key structural facts:
- The only \(T\)-dependence is **linear in \(T\)** and it appears **only multiplied by \(\log(\epsilon+1)\)**.
- There is also a **\(T\)-independent** term \(-2.4819\cdot 337.7690\cdot \log(\epsilon+1)\).

Still has log(T*c5+1) not T. **[NO MATCH]**

= T*c0*epsilon + T*c2/epsilon + (c3+c4)/epsilon + c5*log(c6*epsilon+1)/epsilon² + c7*epsilon + c8*log(c6*epsilon+1)
